   3              	;@"      Filename: smartstart64.s											"

   6              	;@"																			"

   8              	;@"																            "
   9              	;@"     This sourcecode is released for the purpose to promote programming  "
  10              	;@"  on the Raspberry Pi. You may redistribute it and/or modify with the    "

  12              	;@"																            "
  13              	;@"      The SOURCE CODE is distributed "AS IS" WITHOUT WARRANTIES AS TO    "
  14              	;@"   PERFORMANCE OF MERCHANTABILITY WHETHER EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED.          "
  15              	;@"   Redistributions of source code must retain the copyright notices to   "
  16              	;@"   maintain the author credit (attribution) .							"
  17              	;@"																			"
  18              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  19              	;@"                                                                         "
  20              	;@"       This code expands on my earlier SmartStart bootstub assembler for "
  21              	;@" the Pi3. It directly supports multicore operation in C/C++. To do that  "
  22              	;@" it provides stack space to each core and provides a modified bootloader " 
  23              	;@" spinlock that protects against registers X0-X7 trashed. As any C/C++    "
  24              	;@" 64 bit compiler will trash those registers, to use C/C++ in multicore   "
  25              	;@" programming this protection must be done.								"
  26              	;@"       This is a matching paired AARCH64 stub for the 64bit linker file  "
  27              	;@" and carries the samme arrangement as AARCH32 to ease porting.		    "
  28              	;@"																            "
  29              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"*/
  30              	
  31              	.section ".text.startup", "ax", %progbits
  32              	.balign	4
  33              	.globl _start
  34              	_start:	
  35 0000 0C000010 		adr x12, _start							// Hold boot address in high register R12
  36 0004 610D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_BootAddr					// Address of RPi_BootAddr
  37 0008 2C0000B9 		str w12, [x1]							// Store the boot address
  38              	
  39 000c 600D0058 		ldr	x0, =0x3F000000						// No need to detect address in 64bit mode it has to be 0x3F000000 on Pi3
  40 0010 810D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_IO_Base_Addr				// Address of RPi_IO_Base_Addr
  41 0014 200000B9 		str w0, [x1]							// Store the IO base address
  42              	
  43 0018 200080D2 		mov x0, #1								// Multicore support starts as 1 core
  44 001c 610D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_CoresReady					// Address of RPi_CoresReady
  45 0020 200000B9 		str w0, [x1]							// Store the CoresReady count as 1
  46              	
  47 0024 001380D2 		mov x0, #0x98							// Compiled for ARM8 CPU in AARCH64 and supports 4 cores
  48 0028 410D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_CompileMode				// Address of RPi_CompileMode
  49 002c 200000B9 		str w0, [x1]							// Store the compiler mode  
  50              	
  51 0030 000038D5 		mrs	x0, midr_el1						// Read CPU Id register
  52 0034 210D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_CpuId						// Address of RPi_CpuId
  53 0038 200000B9 		str w0, [x1]							// Store the CPU id

  55              	//"================================================================"
  56              	//  Initialize Generic Timers for Core0
  57              	//"================================================================"
  58 003c 00E13CD5 		mrs	x0, cnthctl_el2
  59 0040 000440B2 		orr	x0, x0, #0x3						/* Enable EL1 access to timers */
  60 0044 00E11CD5 		msr	cnthctl_el2, x0

  66 0054 00E118D5 		msr	cntkctl_el1, x0
  67              	
  68              	//"================================================================"
  69              	//  Setup stack pointers for each core and each CPU operation mode
  70              	//"================================================================"
  71              	multicore_start:
  72 0058 420C0058 	    ldr x2, = __EL2_stack_core0				// Address of EL2_stack_core0 stack pointer value
  73 005c 630C0058 	    ldr x3, = __EL1_stack_core0				// Address of EL1_stack_core0 stack pointer value
  74 0060 840C0058 	    ldr x4, = __EL0_stack_core0				// Address of EL0_stack_core0 stack pointer value
  75 0064 A60038D5 		mrs x6, mpidr_el1						// Read core id on ARM8
  76 0068 C60440F2 		ands x6, x6, #0x3						// Make cpu id bitmask
  77 006c C0010054 		beq set_stacks							// Ready to set core 0 stacks
  78 0070 420C0058 	    ldr x2, = __EL2_stack_core1				// Address of EL2_stack_core1 stack pointer value
  79 0074 630C0058 	    ldr x3, = __EL1_stack_core1				// Address of EL1_stack_core1 stack pointer value
  80 0078 840C0058 	    ldr x4, = __EL0_stack_core1				// Address of EL0_stack_core1 stack pointer value
  81 007c DF0400F1 		cmp x6, #1								// Check cpu id for core 1
  82 0080 20010054 		beq set_stacks							// Ready to set core 1 stacks
  83 0084 620C0058 	    ldr x2, = __EL2_stack_core2				// Address of EL2_stack_core2 stack pointer value
  84 0088 830C0058 	    ldr x3, = __EL1_stack_core2				// Address of EL1_stack_core2 stack pointer value
  85 008c A40C0058 	    ldr x4, = __EL0_stack_core2				// Address of EL0_stack_core2 stack pointer value
  86 0090 DF0800F1 		cmp x6, #2								// Check cpu id for core 2
  87 0094 80000054 		beq set_stacks							// Ready to set core 1 stacks
  88 0098 820C0058 	    ldr x2, = __EL2_stack_core3				// Address of EL2_stack_core3 stack pointer value
  89 009c A30C0058 	    ldr x3, = __EL1_stack_core3				// Address of EL1_stack_core3 stack pointer value
  90 00a0 C40C0058 	    ldr x4, = __EL0_stack_core3				// Address of EL0_stack_core3 stack pointer value
  91              	set_stacks:
  92 00a4 5F000091 		mov	sp, x2								/* EL2 stack set */
  93 00a8 03411CD5 		msr	sp_el1, x3							/* EL1 stack set */
  94 00ac 044118D5 		msr	sp_el0, x4							/* EL0 stack set */
  95

  97              	//  Initilize MPID/MPIDR registers for all Cores
  98              	//"================================================================"
  99 00b0 000038D5 		mrs	x0, midr_el1
 100 00b4 A10038D5 		mrs	x1, mpidr_el1
 101 00b8 00001CD5 		msr	vpidr_el2, x0
 102 00bc A1001CD5 		msr	vmpidr_el2, x1

 112              	
 113              	//"================================================================"
 114              	//  Initialize HCR_EL2 so EL1 is 64 bits for all Cores
 115              	//"================================================================"
 116 00d4 0000B0D2 		mov	x0, #(1 << 31)						// 64bit EL1
 117 00d8 00111CD5 		msr	hcr_el2, x0
 118              	
 119              	//"================================================================"
 120              	//  Initialize SCTLR_EL1 for all Cores
 121              	//"================================================================"
 122              	    /*  RES1 bits (29,28,23,22,20,11) to 1
 123              		 *  RES0 bits (31,30,27,21,17,13,10,6) +
 124              		 *  UCI,EE,EOE,WXN,nTWE,nTWI,UCT,DZE,I,UMA,SED,ITD,
 125              		 *  CP15BEN,SA0,SA,C,A,M to 0 */
 126 00dc 000081D2 		mov	x0, #0x0800
 127 00e0 001AA6F2 		movk	x0, #0x30d0, lsl #16
 128 00e4 00007EB2 		orr    x0, x0, #(0x1 << 2)            // The C bit on (data cache). 
 129 00e8 000074B2 		orr    x0, x0, #(0x1 << 12)           // The I bit on (instruction cache)
 130 00ec 001018D5 		msr	sctlr_el1, x0
 131              	
 132              	//"================================================================"
 133              	//  Return to the EL1_SP1 mode from EL2 for all Cores
 134              	//"================================================================"
 135 00f0 A07880D2 		mov	x0, #0x3c5							// EL1_SP1 | D | A | I | F
 136 00f4 00401CD5 		msr	spsr_el2, x0						// Set spsr_el2 with settings
 137 00f8 60000010 		adr	x0, exit_el1						// Address to exit EL2
 138 00fc 20401CD5 		msr	elr_el2, x0							// Set elevated return register
 139 0100 E0039FD6 		eret									// Call elevated return
 140              	exit_el1:
 141 0104 A60038D5 		mrs x6, mpidr_el1						// Read core id on ARM8
 142 0108 C6044092 		and x6, x6, #0x3						// Make cpu id bitmask
 143 010c C60000B4 		cbz x6, cpu0_exit_multicore_park		// Core0 continues on
 144              	
 145              	//"================================================================"
 146              	//      Now park Core 1,2,3 into secondary spinloop on BCM2837
 147              	//"================================================================"
 148 0110 C1050058 		ldr x1, =RPi_CoresReady					// Address of CoreReady count

 174              	//"================================================================"
 175              	//			Core0 will bring Core 1,2,3 to secondary spin 
 176              	//"================================================================"
 177              	#define spin_cpu1 0xe0
 178 0148 011C80D2 		mov x1, #spin_cpu1						// Spin core1 jump address
 179 014c 62080058 		ldr x2, =multicore_start				// Function we are going to call
 180 0150 220000F9 		str	x2, [x1]							// Store the function address to core1
 181 0154 9F2003D5 		sev										// Wake core1 up
 182 0158 83030058 	 	ldr x3, =RPi_CoresReady					// Set CoresReady count address
 183              	.WaitCore1ACK:
 184 015c 610040B9 		ldr	w1, [x3]							// Read CoresReady count
 185 0160 3F080071 		cmp	w1, #2								// Wait for setting of second core ready
 186 0164 C1FFFF54 		bne	.WaitCore1ACK						// Core1 not ready so read again
 187              	#define spin_cpu2 0xe8

 195 0180 3F0C0071 		cmp	w1, #3								// Wait for setting of third core ready
 196 0184 C1FFFF54 		bne	.WaitCore2ACK						// Core2 not ready so read again
 197              	#define spin_cpu3 0xf0

 199 018c 62060058 		ldr x2, =multicore_start				// Function we are going to call
 200 0190 220000F9 		str	x2, [x1]							// Store the function address to core3
 201 0194 9F2003D5 		sev										// Wake core3 up
 202 0198 83010058 	 	ldr x3, =RPi_CoresReady					// Set CoresReady count address
 203              	.WaitCore3ACK:
